# Karvia Business — Audit Tracker

**Single source of truth for all audit findings.**
**Last Updated**: June 2, 2026
**Status**: Active

---

## How This File Works

- Every `/audit` session reads this file first
- New findings are **appended** here (not in separate report files)
- Each finding has a status: `OPEN`, `FIXED`, `DEFERRED`, `WONTFIX`, `LOCKED`
- `/close` after an audit session verifies no duplicate reports were created
- Archived reports live in `2-QA-AND-TESTING/QA/sprints/archive/audit-reports/`

---

## Audit Governance Convention (formalized 2026-05-06)

**Effective forward-only — older entries (`AH-*`, `AM-*`, `AL-*`) keep their existing IDs; not retrofitted.**

### Stable ID scheme
- Format: `A{YYYYMMDD}-{nn}` — e.g., `A20260506-01`
- 11 chars; date-sortable; greppable; never reused
- One ID per *actionable change* that produces a plan amendment
- Drops, deferrals, and "verify-only" findings do NOT get IDs (deferrals listed in inventory section)

### Three-stage status flags per ID
| Flag | Meaning | Set when |
|---|---|---|
| 📝 **PLAN** | Sprint plan amended | `/audit` walkthrough closes |
| 💻 **CODE** | Code shipped + committed | `/coding` session implements; ID cited in commit message |
| ✅ **TESTS** | Regression suite green | Sprint close verifies suite |

An ID is "done" only when all three flags are set. ID stuck at PLAN-only past target sprint's close = unresolved debt → re-audit trigger.

### Three places, one job each
| Place | Role |
|---|---|
| **AUDIT_TRACKER.md** (this file) | Single source of truth — Status Matrix per audit session |
| **Per-sprint handoff doc** (`SPRINT{X}_HANDOFF_DOCUMENT.md`) | Mirror — "Audit History" section listing audit IDs that amended *this* sprint |
| **Audit findings doc** (e.g., `AUDIT_S24_S27_FINDINGS.md`) | The "why" record — IDs cited in Locked Decisions |

### Workflow integration
- `/audit` close: assign IDs · build master Status Matrix · add Audit History to every affected sprint handoff · all flags = PLAN
- `/coding`: when implementing audit-amended item → set CODE flag in both master + sprint · cite ID in commit message
- `/close`: verify all touched IDs have correct flags · surface unresolved IDs in handoff
- `/init`: orphan check — IDs at PLAN-only past their target sprint's close → flag as re-audit trigger

### Deferrals (no IDs)
Items deferred to refinement / post-Beta / feature-owning sprint do NOT get stable IDs (no change to track). Listed in `KARVIA_STRATEGY/3-DELIVERY/1-SPRINTS/REFINEMENT-BACKLOG/README.md` under "Audit-driven deferrals" with category + pointer back to audit doc.

---

- **Category**: Architecture
- **Severity**: HIGH
- **Location**: `server/routes/assessments.js:2526` (`/trends`), `server/routes/assessments.js:2597` (`/compare`)

- **Source**: Sprint 20 Impact Analysis Mar 18
- **Status**: FIXED (Mar 18)
- **Category**: Architecture
- **Severity**: HIGH
- **Location**: SPRINT20_TECHNICAL_SPEC.md API endpoints

## OPEN — Consultant Assessment-View Authorization Bug 2026-05-12 (Session #230)

**Trigger**: User screenshot during S25 close session. Consultant on `karvia-business-1.onrender.com/pages/my-clients.html` clicks the **Assessment** tab for a client → opens `/pages/team-ssi-view.html?client=<id>&from=workspace` → fires alert **"You are not authorized to view this client's assessments."** then leaves the page stuck at "Loading results...". Blocks core consultant workflow (viewing an assigned client's SSI assessment results — the canonical entry into a client's data).

**Deferral**: Per user direction 2026-05-12, **not picked up in Sprint 25**; defer to **post-S25 triage** (Sprint 26 candidate, or refinement-track depending on triage when S25 closes).

**Suspected origin** (not root-caused — repro/triage owed):
- Frontend alert fires from `client/pages/scripts/team-ssi-view.js:54` when `ConsultantPageMode.detect()` returns `mode === 'unauthorized'`.
- Decision lives at `client/js/consultant-page-mode.js:70` — verdict is "unauthorized" when `user.managed_businesses` (read from `karvia_user` localStorage blob) does not contain the URL `?client=<id>`. Comparison at line 69 is `String(id) === String(clientId)` — stringified equality, which rules out ObjectId-vs-string mismatch as the culprit.
- Likely causes to triage (ordered by likelihood): **(a)** `karvia_user` blob is stale and `managed_businesses` is empty/outdated post-login (clients added after the blob was cached → frontend never refetches); **(b)** login response from `POST /api/auth/login` (or `/me`) doesn't include `managed_businesses` at all (server payload gap); **(c)** consultant↔client assignment never persisted to `User.managed_businesses` despite a successful add-client wizard run; **(d)** my-clients.html links use a different id (e.g. `client.company_id` vs `client._id`) than what's stored in `managed_businesses`.
- Server-side enforcement (`requireManagedClient` middleware on consultant routes; `managed_businesses` check at `PUT /api/companies/:id`) is the deeper gate — even if frontend mode is corrected, server must agree. Triage should run both sides.

### Triage outcomes — /audit 2026-05-13 (post-mint)

**A20260513-05 — root REFRAMED**. Both mint-suspicions REFUTED:
- `?assessment=<id>` IS a real `Assessment._id`: [Invitation.assessment_id schema](../../../server/models/Invitation.js#L135-L141) is `ref: 'Assessment'`; [assessments.js:329](../../../server/routes/assessments.js#L329) sets `invitation.assessment_id = assessment._id` right after `assessment.save()`; [`assigned-to-me`](../../../server/routes/invitations.js#L798) surfaces that field directly.
- `/api/assessments/:id/detailed-results` does NOT deny EMPLOYEE owner reads: [assessments.js:1631-1640](../../../server/routes/assessments.js#L1631-L1640) — `isOwner = assessment.user_id._id === user.id` passes through.

**Actual root**: init-flow collision in [team-ssi-view.js:99-113](../../../client/pages/scripts/team-ssi-view.js#L99-L113). `loadCompanyResults()` runs BEFORE `switchTab('my-results')`. For EMPLOYEE it synthesizes `teamResults` from `Company.assessment_scores ÷ 10`; if that rollup is empty/zero on the client (E.1/E.2 backfill gap for THIS specific company), `hasData=false` at [line 538](../../../client/pages/scripts/team-ssi-view.js#L538) → [`showEmptyState()` at line 2295](../../../client/pages/scripts/team-ssi-view.js#L2295) fires → **hides `#tab-container` entirely** → page-level `#empty-state` ("No Assessment Results Yet" at [team-ssi-view.html:398](../../../client/pages/team-ssi-view.html#L398)) overlays before my-results tab renders. Confounder: the in-tab `#my-results-empty` ([html:273](../../../client/pages/team-ssi-view.html#L273)) and page-level `#empty-state` use IDENTICAL copy → indistinguishable from screenshot.

**Minimal fix** (~3-5 LoC FE, [team-ssi-view.js:540](../../../client/pages/scripts/team-ssi-view.js#L540)): gate `showEmptyState()` for EMPLOYEE — EMPLOYEE has a dedicated My Results path, the global empty-state should never overlay them. Let `switchTab('my-results')` paint the tab. Scope guard intact (no template_id routing, no rename, single-template SSI preserved).

**A20260513-06 — root CONFIRMED + companion split**. Mint suspicion correct.
- [team-ssi-view.js:555](../../../client/pages/scripts/team-ssi-view.js#L555) reads `total_completed`/`total_members` from `this.teamResults`, loaded from `GET /api/assessments/company/:id/team-breakdown` at [line 371](../../../client/pages/scripts/team-ssi-view.js#L371).
- [`/team-breakdown` at assessments.js:758-761](../../../server/routes/assessments.js#L758-L761) iterates `Team.find({ company_id, is_active })` and counts members-with-completed-assessment **per Team row**. Companies with 3 Assessment docs but 0 Team rows (BO-only shop / 5-person shop — same E.1 scenario) get `total_completed=0, total_members=0`.
- Canonical data exists at [`/company-results` at line 2236-2243](../../../server/routes/assessments.js#L2236-L2243) — direct `Assessment.find({ company_id, status: { $ne: 'excluded' } })` + dedupe-per-user → returns the correct 3.

**Minimal fix (main)** (~12-15 LoC BE, [server/routes/assessments.js `/team-breakdown` response builder](../../../server/routes/assessments.js#L758)): bypass Team-row gating for the headline count by overwriting `total_completed = distinctUsers.length` (from `Assessment.distinct('user_id', { company_id, status: 'completed', user_id: { $ne: null } })`) and `total_members = User.countDocuments({ company_id, is_active: true, role: { $ne: 'CONSULTANT' } })`. Single source of truth preserved per `feedback_extend_before_wrap` (extends existing endpoint vs. drafting a new aggregator).

**Companion split — A20260513-06b** (sibling miscount, different root): [assessment-hub KPI strip](../../../client/pages/assessment-hub.html#L1124) "Sent: 1 / Completed: 1" reads `/kpi-summary` which for non-CONSULTANT scopes BOTH counts by `sent_by: userId` ([assessments.js:2365 + 2371](../../../server/routes/assessments.js#L2365)). BO sees only her personal sends, not company-wide. Fix: role-condition the `sent_by` filter — drop it for BUSINESS_OWNER + EXECUTIVE (company-wide), keep for MANAGER (personal scope is correct for them). ~6-8 LoC BE. Splitting as `-06b` rather than folding into `-06` because the fix touches a different endpoint and has its own persona semantics.

**Pass-2 on -13/-14/-15/-17/-16(a)**: ✅ all 6 regression scripts present in `scripts/test-sprint26-A20260512-*.js`; [server/config/index.js:294](../../../server/config/index.js#L294) `APP_URL` fail-fast intact (-13). No re-audit action.

**S26/S27 4-persona journey impact**: -05 blocks EMPLOYEE journey (Diagnose→Author handoff broken); -06 main blocks BO/EXEC/MANAGER cockpit credibility; -06b blocks BO/EXEC dashboard credibility. CONSULTANT unaffected by -05 (My Results hidden by design) but affected by -06 main and -06b (verify cross-company scope semantics in /coding). All three are in S26 polish scope — not S27 carry.

## OPEN — Planning Cascade Strategy 2026-05-14 (/strategy session #240, follows B1 /coding)

**Trigger**: Sprint 26 B1 `/coding` (sealed today, 3 commits, 119 new assertions) closed the visible Beta blocker — wizard now creates custom-period objectives with real dates (Slice 2.1), AI prompts inherit objective horizon (Slice 2.2), goal-date hierarchy enforced (Slice 2.4). But the planning cascade BENEATH objectives still anchored on calendar quarters ("Q3 2026" selector on quarterly-goals.html). User direction at /strategy session #240 reframed the conceptual model: **OKRs in Karvia are per-objective projects with arbitrary start + duration, NOT slots in a shared annual cycle**. Consultants onboard clients at any time; each client objective is a project (e.g., "Create org chart" = 3 months from today). No fiscal-year framing applies.

**Deliverable**: [SPRINT26_PLANNING_CASCADE_STRATEGY.md](../1-SPRINTS/SPRINT-26-First-Objective/SPRINT26_PLANNING_CASCADE_STRATEGY.md) — 5 strategic decisions locked (SD-1/2/3/4/5 per user "I clocked the decisions now"); 5 sub-slices specced (2.3.1 schema relaxation → 2.3.2 route writes → 2.3.3 planning page redesign → 2.3.4 Window CRUD + auto-split → 2.3.5 dashboard KPI reframe). Total ~700 LoC code + ~345 LoC tests, ~8h split across 2-3 `/coding` sessions.

**Verdict**: 🟢 GREEN — strategy locked, ready for execution. B3 deferred per user direction ("let's do the coding session later"). Slice 2.3 grew from initial estimate of 1-1.5h to ~8h because the reframe demanded objective-first navigation (kill calendar quarter selector entirely) instead of branched UI.

## OPEN — Manager Team-Visibility + Invite-Permission Gap 2026-05-17 (user-surfaced /testing replay)

**Trigger**: User reported during /testing Gate 4-12 replay session: after BO creates a team and adds a Manager as a member, the Manager logging in sees "No Teams Yet" empty state on `/pages/teams.html` instead of the team. Manager cannot invite Employees because there's no team listed for them to add to. User direction: "Not a bug but something of an improvement -- if member is the manager, the manager when he logs in he should be able to view the team that he has added and he should also be able to invite employees to the same team or create new teams -- so that the flow is not broken."

**Verdict**: 🟡 YELLOW — UX friction confirmed across 2 code layers (visibility + permission); fix scope surfaced (3 options); user direction "file as audit ID" → row minted in 📝 PLAN state, deferred to refinement-track. No code edits this session per `feedback_no_destructive_without_greenlight`.

**Reproduction**: BO logs in, navigates to `/pages/teams.html`, clicks "Create First Team", fills form WITHOUT explicitly selecting a Manager from the dropdown at [client/pages/scripts/teams.js:272-274](../../../client/pages/scripts/teams.js#L272), adds a Manager-role user as a member. Manager logs in → `/pages/teams.html` → empty state "No Teams Yet" + "Create First Team" CTA.

**Root cause (2 layers)**:

| Layer | Surface | Defect |
|---|---|---|
| **Layer 1 — visibility** | [server/routes/teams.js:311](../../../server/routes/teams.js#L311) `GET /api/teams` MANAGER branch | Calls `Team.findByManager(userId)` ([Team.js:277](../../../server/models/Team.js#L277)) which filters by `manager_id === userId` only. Does NOT include teams where user is a member with role=MANAGER. When BO creates without selecting a Manager from the dropdown, `manager_id` defaults to BO's id → Manager added as member sees nothing |
| **Layer 2 — permission** | [server/routes/teams.js:880-887](../../../server/routes/teams.js#L880) `POST /:teamId/members/create-user` permission gate | Also checks `team.manager_id.toString() === currentUser.id`. Even if visibility were fixed, Manager would 403 on invite unless they're literally the `manager_id` |

Both visibility AND permission tied to the single `manager_id` field. The data model assumes 1 manager per team; the UX expectation is "any MANAGER-role member can manage the team."

**Not a dead-end** (workarounds exist):
- BO can select Manager from the dropdown at team-creation time → `manager_id` set to Manager → flow works
- BO can edit team afterward via PUT `/api/teams/:teamId` and reassign `manager_id`

But the default path (BO creates without picking a Manager) silently breaks Manager onboarding.

**Fix options surfaced** (no code touched per `feedback_no_destructive_without_greenlight`):

| Option | Scope | LoC | Trade-off |
|---|---|---|---|
| **(A) Relax MANAGER semantic** — visibility uses `findByManager OR findByMember-with-role-MANAGER`; permission gate adds `isMemberAsManager` check | ~10 LoC across [teams.js:311](../../../server/routes/teams.js#L311) + [teams.js:880](../../../server/routes/teams.js#L880) + new `Team.findByManagerOrMember` helper | small, additive | Multiple Managers per team allowed; matches real org dynamics. Permission model loosens from "one owner" to "any MANAGER-role member" |
| **(B) Force handoff at team-creation** — BO must select Manager from dropdown when creating; fallback auto-assigns `manager_id` to first-added MANAGER-role member | ~15 LoC FE validation + BE auto-assign | preserves single-owner | UX heavier; BO can't create empty team; doesn't help if multiple Managers added later |
| **(C) Schema migration** `manager_id` → `manager_ids[]` array | ~100+ LoC + data migration | clean long-term | Beta-blocker scope-wise; touches every consumer of `manager_id`; defer post-Beta |

**Recommended slice when work resumes**: option (A) — additive, small, matches the actual organizational dynamic. Pre-flight before implementing: grep all consumers of `Team.findByManager` to confirm visibility query callers are OK with the broader result set; grep all consumers of the `isTeamManager` predicate to confirm permission relaxation is safe everywhere.

**Severity rationale**: HIGH (not CRITICAL) — Beta-quality UX friction with documented workarounds, not a security/data issue. Affects every BO who creates a team without picking a Manager from the dropdown (likely default for new BOs who don't know the dropdown exists). Not Beta-blocking — `/testing` Gate 4-12 replay can continue today by having BO explicitly select Manager at team creation.

**Pre-investigation also confirmed**:
- The Manager dropdown at [client/pages/scripts/teams.js:272-274](../../../client/pages/scripts/teams.js#L272) DOES include MANAGER-role users in the company — so the BO-selects path works today, the UX just doesn't make it the default expectation
- The `Team.findByMember` helper at [Team.js:289](../../../server/models/Team.js#L289) already returns teams a user is a member of (used for EMPLOYEE branch) — option (A) can reuse-or-extend this helper per `feedback_extend_before_wrap`
- This issue was NOT surfaced by today's /testing of A20260516-02 because that audit walked the *invitation activation* layer (email → token → password set) not the *post-activation Manager team-management* layer. Different concern, different surface.

## OPEN — Multi-Account Login Bug 2026-05-15 (user-surfaced)

**Trigger**: User reported `stringsounds@gmail.com` exists as **two separate accounts** — BUSINESS_OWNER at one company + EMPLOYEE at another — and normal login can only ever reach one (the older `_id`). Same email, two legitimate Users per multi-tenant schema design; login layer was never built to handle the multi-match case.

**Verdict**: 🟡 YELLOW — bug confirmed across 4 code layers; fix scope surfaced (3 options); user direction "lets fix this later" → row minted in 📝 PLAN state, deferred to post-Beta refinement track. No code edits this session per `feedback_no_destructive_without_greenlight`.

**Reproduction**: any user invited as team member (EMPLOYEE/MANAGER/EXECUTIVE) to Company B who is ALSO a BUSINESS_OWNER of Company A. Second User doc legitimately created via `invitation-accept` (predicate is `{email, company_id}`); login predicate is `{email}` only — non-deterministic match.

**Root cause (4 layers)**:

| Layer | File | Behavior | Verdict |
|---|---|---|---|
| 1 — Schema | [server/models/User.js:301-306](../../../server/models/User.js#L301-L306) | Email unique **per company** via compound index `{company_id, email}` (sparse); globally unique only for CONSULTANT via partial filter | ✅ correct — multi-tenant intent |
| 2 — Signup | [server/routes/auth.js:65](../../../server/routes/auth.js#L65) | `findOne({email})` global — blocks legitimate second-business signup | ❌ contradicts Layer 1 |
| 3 — Login | [server/routes/auth.js:174](../../../server/routes/auth.js#L174) | `findOne({email})` returns oldest `_id` non-deterministically; second account unreachable | ❌ **THE bug** |
| 4 — Invitation accept | [server/routes/invitations.js:229](../../../server/routes/invitations.js#L229) | Predicate is `{email, company_id}` — legitimately creates second User doc | ✅ correct |

**Fix options surfaced (no code touched)**:

| Option | Scope | Size | Trade-off |
|---|---|---|---|
| **A — Account picker at login** | When `User.find({email})` returns >1, respond `accounts: [{company_name, role}, ...]` (no JWT yet); FE renders picker; second POST `/api/auth/login/select-account` issues JWT for chosen `(user_id)`. Layer 2 signup symmetry ships in same slice (drop global `findOne`; replace with multi-company-confirmation UX). | ~80 LoC BE + ~60 FE + ~50 test | Minimal change. Standard SaaS pattern (Slack, Linear). Honors Layer 1 multi-tenant intent. |
| **B — Unified User w/ `companies[]`** | Schema fields ALREADY EXIST at [User.js auth.js:101-107](../../../server/routes/auth.js#L101) (`companies[]`, `current_company_id`, `managed_companies`) but not fully wired. Merge duplicate User docs into one via backfill; JWT carries `current_company_id`; all multi-tenant queries verified. | ~500+ LoC + backfill + 4-layer refactor | Architecturally cleaner; `feedback_extend_before_wrap` honored (extend the canonical model that already half-exists). Big slice. |
| **C — Global email uniqueness** | Make email globally unique; force `+companyA@` etc. | small | ❌ Breaks Layer 1 intent + bad UX. Rejected. |

**Recommended slice when work resumes**: **A first** (closes user-visible bug, ~1-1.5h `/coding`). **B filed as post-Beta refinement-track** (architectural cleanup; not Beta-blocking once A is in). Layer 2 signup symmetry MUST ship bundled with A.

**Security note**: not a data-leak or auth-bypass class — passwords still gate each account individually; users cannot access accounts they don't own. Pure UX/correctness bug for users with >1 account.

### Status Matrix — A20260515-01 (1 ID)

| ID | Group | Sprint | One-liner | 📝 | 💻 | ✅ | Last-updated |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| `A20260515-01` | MULTI-ACCOUNT-LOGIN (HIGH) | **OPEN (deferred)** — target post-Beta refinement track | **Login non-deterministic when same email exists at multiple companies**. Schema intentionally allows it (Layer 1); login + signup don't handle it (Layers 2-3). Repro: `stringsounds@gmail.com` BO@CompanyA + EMPLOYEE@CompanyB → login always lands on oldest `_id` regardless of which account user intended. Fix: Option A (account picker + signup symmetry) ships first; Option B (unified `User.companies[]` model — schema fields already half-wired) filed as post-Beta refinement. ## FIXED — Manager Welcome Email Defect 2026-05-15 (user-surfaced + `/coding` session)

**Trigger**: User walkthrough — BO added a Manager; the Manager received a welcome email reading "From undefined undefined", "added to Tiger Team by undefined undefined", and a "YOUR LOGIN / Password: 996321412af60fd532c8595dd10854e9c3079ac9e39a919f" credentials box.

**Pre-investigation outcome (impact analysis before any edit per `feedback_no_destructive_without_greenlight`)**: 3 distinct defect surfaces surfaced reading `server/routes/teams.js`, `server/routes/invitations.js`, `server/services/mailjetService.js`. User direction "go ahead" with all 6 pre-edit Qs greenlit (a) → bundled as 3 parts under single `A20260515-04` per `feedback_audit_governance` (one ID per actionable change with multiple fix sites; precedent A20260515-02 parts 1-4). Closes [CLEANUP_ACTIVITIES.md item #1](CLEANUP_ACTIVITIES.md) (PARTIAL → DONE) in same commit per `feedback_cleanup_boundary_pattern`.

**Root cause (3 surfaces)**:

| # | Path | Caller | Bug | Severity |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| P1 | BO/Manager adds team member | [teams.js:1000](../../../server/routes/teams.js#L1000) — `manager_name: ${currentUser.first_name} ${currentUser.last_name}` against JWT payload that only carries `{user_id, email, role, company_id, managed_businesses}` | Header/body/footer all interpolate to "undefined undefined" | **Beta-blocker** — what user reported |
| P2 | Consultant invites portfolio team member | [invitations.js:1824](../../../server/routes/invitations.js#L1824) — called non-existent `mailjetService.sendEmail(...)` with positional args against a destructuring template; every send silently threw `TypeError` (swallowed by surrounding try/catch) | **NO email ever delivered** on this entire path | **Beta-blocker** — silent dropper |
| P3 | "Password: 996321…" credentials box | [mailjetService.js:490](../../../server/services/mailjetService.js#L490) — `credentialsBox(to_email, temp_password)` in `getTeamMemberWelcomeTemplate` | Opaque hex token labeled "Password" (per A20260513-08a comment "reset-link flow handles auth") — misleading and useless to type | **UX defect** — already documented as CLEANUP_ACTIVITIES.md item #1 PARTIAL |

**Fix scope (per `feedback_reuse_max` + `feedback_minimal_change_grounding`)**:

- **P1 fix**: fetch inviter via `User.findById(currentUser.id).select('first_name last_name email').lean()` BEFORE the email send; build `managerName` with email local-part fallback. Mirrors [invitations.js:1646](../../../server/routes/invitations.js#L1646) verbatim. **No JWT payload change** — adding fields to JWT would touch 3 sign sites + invalidate live tokens (rejected per `feedback_minimal_change_grounding`).
- **P2 fix**: rewire to canonical `mailjetService.sendTeamMemberWelcomeEmail({...})` object form (same shape as path 1). Reuses already-fetched `consultant` doc (no second DB hit). Uses `company.name` for `team_name` slot since consultant-invite has no team context.
- **P3 fix**: drop `temp_password` from both `sendTeamMemberWelcomeEmail` + `getTeamMemberWelcomeTemplate` signatures; remove `credentialsBox` call from template body; remove "Temporary Password:" from TextPart; remove mock-mode `console.log('Temp password')`; replace with activation paragraph explaining the Get Started CTA. **`A20260513-08a` hotfix preserved** — `tempPassword = crypto.randomBytes(24).toString('hex')` still seeds `password_hash` in both route handlers (the EMAIL leak is what was misleading, not the schema-side seed).

**Pre-edit Q gates honored** (all 6 greenlit (a) per `feedback_no_destructive_without_greenlight`):

| # | Question | Decision |
|---|---|---|
| Q1 | Scope: 1 path or all 3? | (a) Fix all 3 surfaces in one commit + close CLEANUP item #1 |
| Q2 | Inviter lookup: extra DB hit or JWT enrichment? | (a) Per-request `User.findById` (mirrors invitations.js:1646; ~5ms; not hot path) |
| Q3 | Credentials box: remove, relabel, or leave? | (a) Remove entirely — replace with activation paragraph + Get Started CTA |
| Q4 | Fallback when inviter has no first_name? | (a) Email local-part fallback (`email.split('@')[0]`) |
| Q5 | Test depth? | (a) 3 integration sections (one per surface) + anti-regression on A20260513-08a |
| Q6 | Audit ID + commit shape? | (a) Single ID `A20260515-04` with 3 parts; single commit; close CLEANUP item #1 in same commit |

**Verdict**: 🟡 YELLOW — 11 findings (1 CRITICAL + 3 HIGH + 4 MEDIUM + 3 LOW). One CRITICAL is a hardcoded default password fallback live in 3 invitation routes — recommend immediate `/coding-hotfix` per /audit Step 4 (CRITICAL = Fix Immediately). Pre-existing pre-flagged finding from B.2 grounding (`Invitation.js:495`) confirmed + companion `:489` found. No code edits this session per `feedback_no_destructive_without_greenlight` — triage only; each fix mints its own greenlight gate at /coding time.

Each finding cross-checked against current code (line numbers verified at sweep time).

| `A20260513-08d` | HARDCODE-ENGINE-URL (HIGH) | post-Beta polish | **Microservice engine URL fallbacks `process.env.<X>_URL \|\| 'http://localhost:<port>'` in 7 sites.** [server/middleware/authGuards.js:365](../../../server/middleware/authGuards.js#L365), [server/routes/auth.js:15](../../../server/routes/auth.js#L15), [server/routes/objectives.js:11](../../../server/routes/objectives.js#L11) (PLANNER), [server/routes/assessments.js:11](../../../server/routes/assessments.js#L11) (ASSESSMENT), [server/routes/analytics.js:18](../../../server/routes/analytics.js#L18) (SCORING), [server/services/progress-tracker.js:20](../../../server/services/progress-tracker.js#L20), [server/services/cascade-engine.js:19](../../../server/services/cascade-engine.js#L19). - Consultant signup, add-client (auto-fires invitation email), assessment-send (multi-recipient), invitation-accept (creates user + company), assessment-take (start + submit), client-side results view, consultant-side results view, objective creation with embedded KRs, quarterly + weekly goal creation, task creation + assign, task-complete cascade to goal-level (`status='completed'`, `current_value` bump, `metrics.{completed_tasks,completion_rate}` update). - Consultant cannot author objectives directly → covered by S26 Workstream C (consultant initiates / monitors / nudges; deep-links to BO wizard — Group 3a)

## FIXED — Storage-Key Fragmentation Audit (May 7, 2026)

**Trigger**: Production-symptom discovery during S24 #203 dev verification. My Clients page on `karvia-business-1` returned `TOKEN_EXPIRED` 401s on `/portfolio-kpis` + `/portfolio-summary` even after re-login. Root cause traced to `client/pages/scripts/my-clients.js:124-125` reading the legacy `karvia_token` localStorage key BEFORE the canonical `karvia_auth_token`, allowing a stale legacy token (signed correctly with same `JWT_SECRET`, but with `exp` in the past) to shadow the fresh token forever. Re-login replaces `karvia_auth_token` but never `karvia_token`, so the symptom is permanent until the legacy key is manually removed or organically expires past the 7d window.

**Sweep scope** (expanded after initial token-only scan caught further legacy clusters):
- Auth token: `karvia_auth_token` (canonical) vs `karvia_token` (legacy) vs `token` (oldest, unprefixed)
- User blob: `karvia_user` (canonical) vs `user` (legacy)
- Other `karvia_*` keys checked for fragmentation: `karvia_consultant_own_company`, `karvia_remember`, `karvia_ai_knows_expanded` — **all clean** (single name, single read pattern across consumers)

**Method**: Two-pass per key family — (1) read-order audit across all consumers, (2) writer audit to identify which paths perpetuate the legacy key (because if anything still writes the legacy name, the migration never completes).

**Sign-off complete**: shipped same-day in `#204` (commits to follow this status update). All 3 code IDs (`A20260507-01/03/04`) advanced to ✅ TESTS via single regression `scripts/test-sprint24-204-storage-key-cleanup.js` (23 assertions) + full S22+S22a+S23+S24+phase3 sweep 25/25 suites green. Process ID `A20260507-02` remains as audit-checklist amendment.

### Status Matrix — A20260507-* (4 IDs)

| ID | Group | Sprint | One-liner | 📝 | 💻 | ✅ | Last-updated |

| `A20260507-01` | TKF-A | S24 #204 | **Auth-token cluster fix** (`karvia_auth_token` ↔ legacy `karvia_token`): (a) flip read order in `my-clients.js` to `karvia_auth_token` only; (b) remove legacy `setItem('karvia_token', ...)` writes in `common.js` + `navigation.js`; (c) convert `karvia_token`-only readers (`quarterly-review.js`, `dashboard-v2.js`, `signup.html`) to canonical; (d) one-shot `removeItem` cleanup at boot in BOTH `common.js` and `auth-check.js` (idempotent); (e) bulk-strip `\|\| getItem('karvia_token')` fallback chains across all 15 affected files (perl + 2 manual multi-line fixes); (f) regression `scripts/test-sprint24-204-storage-key-cleanup.js` (23 assertions) greps client tree — only migration shim allowed to read legacy keys; zero legacy writes. **Shipped #204** 2026-05-07. | ✓ #203 | ✓ #204 | ✓ #204 (23/23 new + S22+S22a+S23+S24+phase3 sweep 25/25 suites green) | 2026-05-07 |
| `A20260507-02` | TKF-B | Cross-cutting (audit lens, no code) | **Audit-lens gap.** No prior audit swept for "synonymous storage keys with read-order mismatch across consumers." This pattern (legacy + canonical key both written, read-order varying by file) creates invisible shadow-state bugs that survive logout/login cycles because `localStorage.removeItem` typically targets the canonical key only. Add to future `/audit` checklist: for every pair of synonymous storage keys (cookie / localStorage / sessionStorage), (1) assert exactly one writer per key, (2) assert read-order is identical across all consumers, (3) assert no current code writes the legacy key (otherwise migration never completes). Same rule applies to query-param synonyms (`?client=X` vs `?company=X`), header synonyms, and DB-field synonyms during schema migrations. | ✓ #203 | n/a (process — bake into `/audit` skill prompt) | n/a | 2026-05-07 |

Boot cleanup `removeItem('user')` added in both `common.js` and `auth-check.js`. Regression test asserts ZERO `getItem('user')` reads anywhere in client tree. **Shipped #204** 2026-05-07. | ✓ #203 | ✓ #204 | ✓ #204 (covered by same regression test) | 2026-05-07 |
| `A20260507-04` | TKF-D | S24 #204 — bundled with A20260507-01 | **Bare-`token` 3rd-tier legacy fix.** Dropped `\|\| getItem('token')` 3rd-tier from all 5 fallback chains (`auth-check.js`, `common.js`, `my-clients.js`, `add-client-wizard.js` — `common.js` had it twice). **Legend**: ✓ = flag set · — = pending · ✗ = blocked · n/a = not applicable to this finding type. Update master + per-sprint Audit History when CODE / TESTS flags advance.

### Audit risk register — what this miss tells us

| Risk | Why it slipped past prior audits | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| **Shadow-state from legacy keys** | Audits inspect "is the key being read correctly?" but not "is read-order consistent across N consumers?" When N=1 a bug is visible; with N≥2 and inconsistent ordering, the bug only fires for users whose localStorage holds BOTH keys (rare in dev, common after a key-rename migration in prod) | Add `phase3-X` lint script that greps `getItem(X)` patterns and asserts ordering uniformity. Run in CI like `phase3-3-frontend-role-checks.js`. |
| **Compat-shim writers outliving migration** | "Write both keys for a release, then remove" pattern is correct in theory but has no scheduled cleanup; the dual-write becomes permanent | Every dual-write add must come with a removal commit scheduled in the next sprint. Track via stable audit ID (this is what `A20260507-01` step (b) does). |
| **Production-only repro** | Dev environment usually has clean localStorage; the user with the longest session history hits the bug first. Low test-coverage signal. | Ensure regression tests seed BOTH keys with mismatched expirations and verify canonical wins. (Step (e) of `A20260507-01`.) |
| **"Token has expired" misleading error** | The error message accurately reports `TokenExpiredError` from jwt.verify, but it MASKS the real cause (read order). The user re-logs in, the symptom persists, the real cause is invisible without server logs + decoding the stored token. | Consider augmenting the auth middleware error with a hint: when `TokenExpiredError` fires repeatedly for the same user within 5 min of a fresh login, log `[auth] suspected stale-token shadow — check client read-order` server-side. (Optional polish; not in `A20260507-01` scope.) |

### Linked deferrals — none

This cluster is fully actionable in Session G; no items split out to refinement.

## OPEN — CI/Process Gate Posture for Paid Users on `development` 2026-05-18 (/audit session)

**Trigger**: User-surfaced concern after process audit revealed paid users on karvia-business-1.onrender.com are receiving direct pushes to `development` with no CI gate, no PR review, and no commit-level guards. 2026 YTD evidence: **210 commits hit `development` from 2026-04-01..2026-05-18 with 0 PRs** across any base branch (vs 18 PRs into main pre-April). Same window: ~25× increase in Claude-assisted token volume on this project (per local-transcript audit), so the period with the most AI-assisted code change had the least review. Branch named "development" is functionally a release branch but configured as a sandbox.

**Deliverable**: 7 audit IDs minted in 📝 PLAN state. Recommended remediation is **3 line-edits across 2 existing files + 1 user-only Render dashboard change** (full risk profile in this /audit's HTML comment journal entry near top of file). No new workflows, no new scripts, no new hook files — extend existing `.github/workflows/test.yml` + `.git/hooks/pre-commit` per `feedback_extend_before_wrap`.

**Verdict**: 🔴 RED on the **single load-bearing finding A20260518-08** (Render auto-deploy bypasses CI — user-only dashboard change required, no agent path). Without that, the entire remediation chain is decorative. 🟡 AMBER on -05/-06/-07 (fix-paths clear, sequencing matters per `feedback_minimal_change_grounding`). 🟢 GREEN on -09/-10/-11 (governance hygiene; mechanical fixes).

### Status Matrix — A20260518-05..-11 /audit (7 IDs)

| ID | Group | Sprint | One-liner | 📝 | 💻 | ✅ | Last-updated |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| `A20260518-05` | DEV-CI-GATE-MISSING (CRITICAL) | S26 process | **`security-tests` + `e2e-tests` jobs in [test.yml:116,159](../../../.github/workflows/test.yml#L116) `if:`-gated to pre-prod/production only.** Paid users on karvia-business-1 receive every push; only unit + integration run on dev. Existing `test:multi-tenant`/`test:golden-path`/`test:consultant` scripts ready but unused on dev pushes. Fix: add `development` to `if:` clauses (no new test code per `feedback_reuse_max`). Currently coincidentally in sync (return to baseline). Fix: /close-time invariant "Summary date = latest comment date".
